\n        // Speech Recognition\n        if ('webkitSpeechRecognition' in window || 'SpeechRecognition' in window) {\n            const SR = window.SpeechRecognition ||     recog.onresult = (e) => {\n                let interim = '', final = '';\n                for (let i = e.resultIndex; i < e.results.length; i++) {\n                    const t = Please type below.';\n        }\n        \n        function toggleMic() {\n            if (isRec) stopMic();\n            else startMic();\n        }\n        \n        function startMic() {\n            if (!recog) {\n                alert('Voice not supported. async (req, res) => {\n    try {\n        const { user_type, raw_transcript, page_route, interaction_mode } = req.body;\n        \n        console.log(`[LEDGER] ${user_type}: \"${raw_transcript}\"`);\n        \n        // Simple analysis\n        const analysis = analyzeText(raw_transcript);\n        \n        // Get TTS response\n        const tts = await getTTSResponse(analysis, user_type);\n        \n        // Insert into global ledger\n        const ledgerRes = await pool.query(`\n            INSERT INTO global_interaction_ledger \n            (user_type, raw_transcript, page_route, interaction_mode, sentiment, emotion, intent, empathy_score)\n            VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5, $6, $7, $8)\n            RETURNING id\n        `, [user_type, raw_transcript, page_route || '/', interaction_mode || 'voice',\n            analysis.sentiment, analysis.emotion, analysis.intent, analysis.empathyScore]);\n        \n        // If boss, also insert into boss_voice_inputs\n        if (user_type === 'boss') {\n            await pool.query(`\n                INSERT INTO boss_voice_inputs (raw_text, processed, action_taken, priority)\n                VALUES ($1, false, '', 'normal')\n            `, [raw_transcript]);\n        }\n        \n        // Update learning stats\n        await pool.query(`\n            UPDATE learning_stats SET \n                total_interactions = COALESCE(total_interactions, 0) + 1,\n                ledger_entries = COALESCE(ledger_entries, 0) + 1,\n                boss_inputs = boss_inputs + CASE WHEN $1 = 'boss' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END,\n                team_inputs = team_inputs + CASE WHEN $1 = 'dev_team' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END,\n                tts_responses_given = COALESCE(tts_responses_given, 0) + catch (e) {\n        console.error('Ledger error:', e);\n        res.status(500).json({ error: e.message });\n    }\n});\n\n// \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n// TEXT ANALYSIS\n// \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\nfunction analyzeText(text) {\n    const lower = text.toLowerCase();\n    \n    // Sentiment\n    const positiveWords = ['good', 'great', 'excellent', 'amazing', 'love', 'happy', 'thanks', 'please', 'awesome', 'perfect', 'wonderful'];\n    const negativeWords = ['bad', 'terrible', 'hate', 'angry', 'frustrated', 'annoying', 'wrong', 'problem', 'issue', 'broken'];\n    \n    const posCount = positiveWords.filter(w => lower.includes(w)).length;\n    const negCount = negativeWords.filter(w => lower.includes(w)).length;\n    \n    let sentiment = 'neutral';\n    if (posCount > negCount) sentiment = 'positive';\n    else if (negCount > posCount) sentiment = 'negative';\n    \n    // Emotion\n    let emotion = 'neutral';\n    if (lower.includes('?') || lower.includes('what') || lower.includes('how') || lower.includes('why')) emotion = 'curiosity';\n    else if (lower.includes('!') || lower.includes('wow') || lower.includes('amazing')) emotion = 'excitement';\n    else if (negCount > 0) emotion = 'frustration';\n    else if (posCount > 0) emotion = 'satisfaction';\n    \n    // Intent\n    let intent = 'general';\n    if (lower.includes('show') || lower.includes('open') || lower.includes('go to') || lower.includes('navigate')) intent = 'navigation';\n    else if (lower.includes('search') || lower.includes('find') || lower.includes('look for')) intent = 'search';\n    else if (lower.includes('help') || lower.includes('how do')) intent = 'help';\n    else if (lower.includes('buy') || lower.includes('purchase') || lower.includes('price')) intent = 'transaction';\n    else if (lower.includes('property') || lower.includes('house') || lower.includes('real estate')) intent = 'property_search';\n    \n    // Empathy score\n    const empathyScore = 0.5 + (posCount * 0.1) - (negCount * 0.15);\n    \n    return { sentiment, emotion, intent, empathyScore: Math.max(0, Math.min(1, empathyScore)) };\n}\n\n// \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n// TTS RESPONSE\n// \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\nasync function getTTSResponse(analysis, userType) {\n    try {\n        const res = await pool.query(`\n            SELECT response_text, response_tone FROM tts_responses\n            WHERE (trigger_type = 'emotion' AND trigger_value = $1)\n               OR (trigger_type = 'intent' AND trigger_value = $2)\n               OR (trigger_type = 'user_type' AND trigger_value = $3)\n            ORDER BY priority DESC LIMIT 1\n        `, [analysis.emotion, analysis.intent, userType]);\n        \n        if (res.rows[0]) {\n            return { text: res.rows[0].response_text, tone: res.rows[0].response_tone };\n        }\n        \n        // Default responses\n        const defaults = {\n            boss: \"Got it, boss. I'm on it.\",\n            dev_team: \"Understood. Processing your request.\",\n            vendor: \"Thank you! I'll help you with that.\",\n            default: \"I understand. How can I help you further?\"\n        };\n        \n        return { text: defaults[userType] || defaults.default, tone: 'helpful' };\n    } catch (e) {\n        return { text: \"I'm listening. How can I help?\", tone: 'neutral' };\n    }\n}\n\n// \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n// PATTERN LEARNING\n// \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\nasync function learnPattern(text, analysis) {\n    try {\n        // Check if similar pattern exists\n        const existing = await pool.query(`\n            SELECT id, occurrence_count FROM learned_patterns\n            WHERE pattern_name ILIKE $1 OR pattern_text ILIKE $1\n            LIMIT 1\n        `, [`%${text.substring(0, 20)}%`]);\n        \n        if (existing.rows[0]) {\n            await pool.query(`\n                UPDATE learned_patterns SET occurrence_count = occurrence_count + 1, last_seen = NOW()\n                WHERE id = $1\n            `, [existing.rows[0].id]);\n        } else if (text.length > 5) {\n            await pool.query(`\n                INSERT INTO learned_patterns (pattern_name, pattern_text, pattern_type, occurrence_count)\n                VALUES ($1, $2, $3, 1)\n            `, [text.substring(0, 50), text, analysis.intent]);\n            \n            await pool.query(`\n                UPDATE learning_stats SET patterns_learned = COALESCE(patterns_learned, 0) + 1 WHERE stat_date = CURRENT_DATE\n            `);\n        }\n    } catch (e) {\n        console.error('Pattern learning error:', e);\n    }\n}\n\n// \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n// API ENDPOINTS\n// \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n\n// Feed\napp.get('/api/feed', async (req, res) => {\n    try {\n        const r = await pool.query(`SELECT * FROM realtime_feed ORDER BY created_at DESC LIMIT 20`);\n        res.json(r.rows);\n    } catch (e) { res.json([]); }\n});\n\n// Crawled sites\napp.get('/api/crawled-sites', async (req, res) => {\n    try {\n        const r = await pool.query(`SELECT * FROM crawled_sources ORDER BY pages_crawled DESC LIMIT 20`);\n        res.json(r.rows);\n    } catch (e) { res.json([]); }\n});\n\n// Patterns\napp.get('/api/patterns', async (req, res) => {\n    try {\n        const r = await pool.query(`SELECT * FROM learned_patterns ORDER BY occurrence_count DESC LIMIT 20`);\n        res.json(r.rows);\n    } catch (e) { res.json([]); }\n});\n\n// Voice {\n        const r = await pool.query(`SELECT * FROM boss_voice_inputs ORDER BY created_at DESC LIMIT 20`);\n        res.json(r.rows);\n    } catch (e) { res.json([]); }\n});\n\n// \"\"\necho \"\ud83d\udcca STEP 3: Ensuring database tables...\"\n\npsql -d $DB_NAME << 'SQLEOF'\n-- Ensure boss_voice_inputs exists\nCREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS boss_voice_inputs (\n    id SERIAL page_route VARCHAR(255),\n    interaction_mode VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'voice',\n    sentiment VARCHAR(50),\n    emotion VARCHAR(50),\n    intent VARCHAR(100),\n    empathy_score DECIMAL(5,4),\n    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW()\n);\n\n-- Ensure learned_patterns exists\nCREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS learned_patterns (\n    id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,\n    pattern_name VARCHAR(100),\n    pattern_text TEXT,\n    pattern_type VARCHAR(50),\n    occurrence_count INTEGER DEFAULT 1,\n    last_seen TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW(),\n    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW()\n);\n\n-- Ensure today's learning_stats row exists\nINSERT INTO learning_stats (stat_date) \nSELECT CURRENT_DATE WHERE NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM learning_stats WHERE stat_date = CURRENT_DATE);\n\nSELECT 'Tables ready' as status;\nSQLEOF\n\necho \"   \u2705 Database patch\n#\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\necho \"\"\necho \"\ud83d\udd17 STEP 6: Creating frontend integration...\"\n\nmkdir -p \"$VV_HOME/frontend/src/utils\"\n\ncat > \"$VV_HOME/frontend/src/utils/agenticAPI.ts\" << 'APIEOF'\n/**\n * VISTAVIEW AGENTIC API\n * Import this in MrVAssistant.tsx to connect to backend\n */\n\nconst AGENTIC_API = 'http://localhost:1117/api';\n\nexport async function sendToAgentic(text: string, userType: string = \\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\napp.post('/api/ledger/log', async (req, res) => {\\n    try {\\n        const { user_type, raw_transcript, page_route, interaction_mode } = req.body;\\n        \\n        console.log(`[LEDGER] ${user_type}: \\\"${raw_transcript}\\\"`);\\n        \\n        // Simple analysis\\n        const analysis = analyzeText(raw_transcript);\\n        \\n        // Get TTS response\\n        const tts = await getTTSResponse(analysis, user_type);\\n        \\n        // Insert into global ledger\\n        const ledgerRes = await pool.query(`\\n            INSERT INTO global_interaction_ledger \\n            (user_type, raw_transcript, page_route, interaction_mode, sentiment, emotion, intent, empathy_score)\\n            VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5, $6, $7, $8)\\n            RETURNING id\\n        `, [user_type, raw_transcript, page_route || '/', interaction_mode || 'voice',\\n            analysis.sentiment, analysis.emotion, analysis.intent, analysis.empathyScore]);\\n        \\n        // If boss, also insert into boss_voice_inputs\\n        if (user_type === 'boss') {\\n            await pool.query(`\\n                INSERT INTO boss_voice_inputs (raw_text, processed, action_taken, priority)\\n                VALUES ($1, false, '', 'normal')\\n            `, [raw_transcript]);\\n        }\\n        \\n        // Update learning stats\\n        await pool.query(`\\n            UPDATE learning_stats SET \\n                total_interactions = COALESCE(total_interactions, 0) + 1,\\n                ledger_entries = COALESCE(ledger_entries, 0) + 1,\\n                boss_inputs = boss_inputs + CASE WHEN $1 = 'boss' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END,\\n                team_inputs = team_inputs + CASE WHEN $1 = 'dev_team' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END,\\n                tts_responses_given = COALESCE(tts_responses_given, 0) + 1,\\n                updated_at = NOW()\\n            WHERE stat_date = CURRENT_DATE\\n        `, [user_type]);\\n        \\n        // Add to realtime feed\\n        await pool.query(`\\n            INSERT INTO realtime_feed (feed_type, title, description, user_type, icon, page_context)\\n            VALUES ('voice_input', $1, $2, $3, '\\ud83c\\udfa4', $4)\\n        `, [`${user_type}: \\\"${raw_transcript.substring(0, 40)}\\\"`, `${analysis.intent} | ${analysis.sentiment}`, user_type, page_route]);\\n        \\n        // Try to learn pattern\\n        await learnPattern(raw_transcript, analysis);\\n        \\n        res.json({\\n            success: true,\\n            ledger_id: ledgerRes.rows[0]?.id,\\n            analysis,\\n            tts_response: tts\\n        });\\n        \\n    } catch (e) {\\n        console.error('Ledger error:', e);\\n        res.status(500).json({ error: e.message });\\n    }\\n});\\n\\n// \\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\n// TEXT ANALYSIS\\n// \\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\nfunction analyzeText(text) {\\n    const lower = text.toLowerCase();\\n    \\n    // Sentiment\\n    const positiveWords = ['good', 'great', 'excellent', 'amazing', 'love', 'happy', 'thanks', 'please', 'awesome', 'perfect', 'wonderful'];\\n    const negativeWords = ['bad', 'terrible', 'hate', 'angry', 'frustrated', 'annoying', 'wrong', 'problem', 'issue', 'broken'];\\n    \\n    const posCount = positiveWords.filter(w => lower.includes(w)).length;\\n    const negCount = negativeWords.filter(w => lower.includes(w)).length;\\n    \\n    let sentiment = 'neutral';\\n    if (posCount > negCount) sentiment = 'positive';\\n    else if (negCount > posCount) sentiment = 'negative';\\n    \\n    // Emotion\\n    let emotion = 'neutral';\\n    if (lower.includes('?') || lower.includes('what') || lower.includes('how') || lower.includes('why')) emotion = 'curiosity';\\n    else if (lower.includes('!') || lower.includes('wow') || lower.includes('amazing')) emotion = 'excitement';\\n    else if (negCount > 0) emotion = 'frustration';\\n    else if (posCount > 0) emotion = 'satisfaction';\\n    \\n    // Intent\\n    let intent = 'general';\\n    if (lower.includes('show') || lower.includes('open') || lower.includes('go to') || lower.includes('navigate')) intent = 'navigation';\\n    else if (lower.includes('search') || lower.includes('find') || lower.includes('look for')) intent = 'search';\\n    else if (lower.includes('help') || lower.includes('how do')) intent = 'help';\\n    else if (lower.includes('buy') || lower.includes('purchase') || lower.includes('price')) intent = 'transaction';\\n    else if (lower.includes('property') || lower.includes('house') || lower.includes('real estate')) intent = 'property_search';\\n    \\n    // Empathy score\\n    const empathyScore = 0.5 + (posCount * 0.1) - (negCount * 0.15);\\n    \\n    return { sentiment, emotion, intent, empathyScore: Math.max(0, Math.min(1, empathyScore)) };\\n}\\n\\n// \\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\n// TTS RESPONSE\\n// \\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\nasync function getTTSResponse(analysis, userType) {\\n    try {\\n        const res = await pool.query(`\\n            SELECT response_text, response_tone FROM tts_responses\\n            WHERE (trigger_type = 'emotion' AND trigger_value = $1)\\n               OR (trigger_type = 'intent' AND trigger_value = $2)\\n               OR (trigger_type = 'user_type' AND trigger_value = $3)\\n            ORDER BY priority DESC LIMIT 1\\n        `, [analysis.emotion, analysis.intent, userType]);\\n        \\n        if (res.rows[0]) {\\n            return { text: res.rows[0].response_text, tone: res.rows[0].response_tone };\\n        }\\n        \\n        // Default responses\\n        const defaults = {\\n            boss: \\\"Got it, boss. I'm on it.\\\",\\n            dev_team: \\\"Understood. Processing your request.\\\",\\n            vendor: \\\"Thank you! I'll help you with that.\\\",\\n            default: \\\"I understand. How can I help you further?\\\"\\n        };\\n        \\n        return { text: defaults[userType] || defaults.default, tone: 'helpful' };\\n    } catch (e) {\\n        return { text: \\\"I'm listening. How can I help?\\\", tone: 'neutral' };\\n    }\\n}\\n\\n// \\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\n// PATTERN LEARNING\\n// \\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\nasync function learnPattern(text, analysis) {\\n    try {\\n        // Check if similar pattern exists\\n        const existing = await pool.query(`\\n            SELECT id, occurrence_count FROM learned_patterns\\n            WHERE pattern_name ILIKE $1 OR pattern_text ILIKE $1\\n            LIMIT 1\\n        `, [`%${text.substring(0, 20)}%`]);\\n        \\n        if (existing.rows[0]) {\\n            await pool.query(`\\n                UPDATE learned_patterns SET occurrence_count = occurrence_count + 1, last_seen = NOW()\\n                WHERE id = $1\\n            `, [existing.rows[0].id]);\\n        } else if (text.length > 5) {\\n            await pool.query(`\\n                INSERT INTO learned_patterns (pattern_name, pattern_text, pattern_type, occurrence_count)\\n                VALUES ($1, $2, $3, 1)\\n            `, [text.substring(0, 50), text, analysis.intent]);\\n            \\n            await pool.query(`\\n                UPDATE learning_stats SET patterns_learned = COALESCE(patterns_learned, 0) + 1 WHERE stat_date = CURRENT_DATE\\n            `);\\n        }\\n    } catch (e) {\\n        console.error('Pattern learning error:', e);\\n    }\\n}\\n\\n// \\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\n// API ENDPOINTS\\n// \\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\n\\n// Feed\\napp.get('/api/feed', async (req, res) => {\\n    try {\\n        const r = await pool.query(`SELECT * FROM realtime_feed ORDER BY created_at DESC LIMIT 20`);\\n        res.json(r.rows);\\n    } catch (e) { res.json([]); }\\n});\\n\\n// Crawled sites\\napp.get('/api/crawled-sites', async (req, res) => {\\n    try {\\n        const r = await pool.query(`SELECT * FROM crawled_sources ORDER BY pages_crawled DESC LIMIT 20`);\\n        res.json(r.rows);\\n    } catch (e) { res.json([]); }\\n});\\n\\n// Patterns\\napp.get('/api/patterns', async (req, res) => {\\n    try {\\n        const r = await pool.query(`SELECT * FROM learned_patterns ORDER BY occurrence_count DESC LIMIT 20`);\\n        res.json(r.rows);\\n    } catch (e) { res.json([]); }\\n});\\n\\n// Voice commands\\napp.get('/api/voice-commands', async (req, res) => {\\n    try {\\n        const r = await pool.query(`SELECT * FROM voice_command_learning ORDER BY times_used DESC LIMIT 20`);\\n        res.json(r.rows);\\n    } catch (e) { res.json([]); }\\n});\\n\\n// Empathy patterns\\napp.get('/api/empathy-patterns', async (req, res) => {\\n    try {\\n        const r = await pool.query(`SELECT * FROM empathy_learning ORDER BY times_used DESC LIMIT 20`);\\n        res.json(r.rows);\\n    } catch (e) { res.json([]); }\\n});\\n\\n// Boss inputs\\napp.get('/api/boss-inputs', async (req, res) => {\\n    try {\\n        const r = await pool.query(`SELECT * FROM boss_voice_inputs ORDER BY created_at DESC LIMIT 20`);\\n        res.json(r.rows);\\n    } catch (e) { res.json([]); }\\n});\\n\\n// Audit\\napp.get('/api/audit', async (req, res) => {\\n    try {\\n        const r = await pool.query(`SELECT * FROM audit_trail ORDER BY created_at DESC LIMIT 20`);\\n        res.json(r.rows);\\n    } catch (e) { res.json([]); }\\n});\\n\\n// Dashboard HTML\\napp.get('/dashboard', (req, res) => {\\n    res.sendFile(path.join(__dirname, 'dashboard.html'));\\n});\\n\\n// Root\\napp.get('/', (req, res) => {\\n    res.redirect('/dashboard');\\n});\\n\\n// \\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\n// \\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\napp.listen(PORT, () => {\\n    console.log('\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550');\\n    console.log('  \\ud83c\\udfe0 VISTAVIEW AGENTIC AI SERVER v32.0');\\n '').toLowerCase();\n    \n    const posWords = ['good', 'great', 'excellent', 'amazing', 'love', 'happy', 'thanks', 'please', 'awesome', 'perfect'];\n    const negWords = ['bad', 'terrible', 'hate', 'angry', 'frustrated', 'annoying', 'wrong', 'problem', 'issue'];\n    \n    const pos = posWords.filter(w => lower.includes(w)).length;\n    const neg = negWords.filter(w => lower.includes(w)).length;\n    \n    let sentiment = 'neutral';\n    if (pos > neg) sentiment = 'positive';\n    else if (neg > pos) sentiment = 'negative';\n    \n    let emotion = 'neutral';\n    if (lower.includes('?')) emotion = 'curiosity';\n    else if (lower.includes('!')) emotion = 'excitement';\n    else if (neg > 0) emotion = 'frustration';\n    else if (pos > 0) emotion = 'satisfaction';\n    \n    let intent = 'general';\n    if (lower.match(/show|open|go to|navigate/)) intent = 'navigation';\n    else if (lower.match(/search|find|look/)) intent = 'search';\n    else if (lower.match(/help|how do/)) intent = 'help';\n    else if (lower.match(/property|house|real estate/)) intent = 'property_search';\n    \n    return { sentiment, emotion, intent, empathyScore: Math.min(1, 0.5 + pos * 0.1 - neg * 0.1) };\n}\n\n// TTS response\nasync function getTTSResponse(analysis, userType) {\n    const responses = {\n        boss: \"Got it, boss. const tablesRes = await pool.query(`\n            SELECT table_name as name, \n                   (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM information_schema.columns WHERE table_name = t.table_name) as columns\n    }\n        }\n        \n        // Sort by count descending\n        tables.sort((a, b) => b.count - a.count);\n        \n        res.json({ stats, tables });\n    } catch (e) {\n       console.log(`[DB] New pattern learned`);\\n            }\\n        }\\n        \\n        // COMMIT\\n        await client.query('COMMIT');\\n        console.log(`[DB] Transaction committed e.message);\\n        res.status(500).json({ error: e.message });\\n    } finally {\\n        client.release();\\n    }\\n});\\n\\n// Text analysis\\nfunction analyzeText(text) {\\n    const lower = (text || '').toLowerCase();\\n    \\n    const posWords = ['good', 'great', 'excellent', 'amazing', 'love', 'happy', 'thanks', 'please', 'awesome', 'perfect'];\\n    const negWords = ['bad', 'terrible', 'hate', 'angry', 'frustrated', 'annoying', 'wrong', 'problem', 'issue'];\\n    \\n    const pos = posWords.filter(w => lower.includes(w)).length;\\n    const neg = negWords.filter(w => lower.includes(w)).length;\\n    \\n    let sentiment = 'neutral';\\n    if (pos > neg) sentiment = 'positive';\\n    else if (neg > pos) sentiment = 'negative';\\n    \\n    let emotion = 'neutral';\\n    if (lower.includes('?')) emotion = 'curiosity';\\n    else if (lower.includes('!')) emotion = 'excitement';\\n    else if (neg > 0) emotion = 'frustration';\\n    else if (pos > 0) emotion = 'satisfaction';\\n    \\n    let intent = 'general';\\n    if (lower.match(/show|open|go to|navigate/)) intent = 'navigation';\\n    else if (lower.match(/search|find|look/)) intent = 'search';\\n    else if (lower.match(/help|how do/)) intent = 'help';\\n    else if (lower.match(/property|house|real estate/)) intent = 'property_search';\\n    \\n    return { sentiment, emotion, intent, empathyScore: Math.min(1, 0.5 + pos * 0.1 - neg * 0.1) };\\n}\\n\\n// TTS response\\nasync function getTTSResponse(analysis, userType) {\\n    const responses = {\\n        boss: \\\"Got it, I'll assist you with your construction needs.\\\",\\n        buyer: \\\"I'll help you find the perfect property!\\\",\\n        default: \\\"I understand. How can I help you further?\\\"\\n    };\\n    return { text: responses[userType] || responses.default, tone: 'helpful' };\\n}\\n\\n//
